<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">ITEM 2.02</font></b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b>RESULTS OF OPERATIONS AND FINANCIAL CONDITION.</b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:27.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">On July&nbsp;23, 2015, Celgene Corporation issued a press release announcing its financial results for its fiscal quarter ended June&nbsp;30, 2015.&#160; A copy of this press release is attached hereto as Exhibit&nbsp;99.1 and is incorporated herein by reference.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:27.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In accordance with General Instruction B.2 of Form&nbsp;8-K, the information in this Current Report on Form&nbsp;8-K, including Exhibit&nbsp;99.1, that is furnished pursuant to this Item 2.02 shall not be deemed to be &#147;filed&#148; for the purposes of Section&nbsp;18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended (the &#147;Exchange Act&#148;), or otherwise subject to the liabilities of that section, and shall not be incorporated by reference into any registration statement or other document filed under the Securities Act of 1933, as amended, or the Exchange Act, except as shall be expressly set forth by specific reference in such filing.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">ITEM 9.01&#160; FINANCIAL STATEMENTS AND EXHIBITS.</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 99.0pt;text-indent:-1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(d)&nbsp;</font>Exhibit&nbsp;99.1<font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Press Release dated July&nbsp;23, 2015 announcing results for the quarter ended June&nbsp;30, 2015.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 121.5pt;text-indent:-94.5pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This exhibit is furnished pursuant to Item 2.02 and shall not be deemed to be &#147;filed.&#148;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">CELGENE REPORTS SECOND QUARTER 2015</font></b></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">OPERATING AND FINANCIAL RESULTS</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#150;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><i>REVLIMID</i><i><font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;font-style:italic;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">&#174;</font></i><i>&#160;Net Product Sales $1,444 Million; Increased 19% Y/Y</i></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#150;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><i>POMALYST</i><i><font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;font-style:italic;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">&#174;</font></i><i>/IMNOVID</i><i><font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;font-style:italic;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">&#174;</font></i><i>&#160;Net Product Sales $235 Million; Increased 46% Y/Y</i></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#150;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><i>ABRAXANE</i><i><font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;font-style:italic;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">&#174;</font></i><i>&#160;Net Product Sales $244 Million; Increased 13% Y/Y</i></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#150;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><i>OTEZLA</i><i><font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;font-style:italic;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">&#174;</font></i><i>&#160;Net Product Sales $90 Million</i></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">SUMMIT, NJ &#151; (July&nbsp;23, 2015) &#151; </font></b>Celgene Corporation (NASDAQ: CELG) reported net product sales of $2,254 million for the second quarter of 2015, a 22 percent increase from the same period in 2014.&#160; The negative net impact of currency on net product sales was 2 percent.&#160; Second quarter total revenue increased 22 percent to $2,278 million compared to $1,873 million in the second quarter of 2014.&#160; Adjusted net income for the second quarter of 2015 increased 36 percent to $1,019 million compared to $748 million in the second quarter of 2014.&#160; Adjusted diluted earnings per share (EPS) in the second quarter of 2015 was $1.23 which includes a $0.06 gain related to the sale of an equity investment upon completion of their acquisition by another company.&#160; For the same period in 2014, adjusted diluted EPS was $0.90.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Based on U.S. GAAP (Generally Accepted Accounting Principles), Celgene reported second quarter of 2015 net income of $356 million or $0.43 per diluted share.&#160; For the second quarter of 2014, net income was $598 million or $0.72 per diluted share.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;The Celgene team delivered exceptional results across the portfolio in the second quarter,&#148; said Bob Hugin, Chairman and Chief Executive Officer of Celgene Corporation.&#160; &#147;We continue to invest strategically in the long-term future of Celgene and expect our recently announced transactions with AstraZeneca, Juno and Receptos to accelerate our earnings growth beginning in 2019.&#148;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade align="left" style="color:#010101;"></div>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Second Quarter 2015 Financial Highlights</font></u></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Unless otherwise stated, all comparisons are for the second quarter of 2015 compared to the second quarter of 2014.&#160; The adjusted operating expense categories presented below exclude share-based employee compensation expense and upfront collaboration payments.&#160; Please see the attached Reconciliation of GAAP to Adjusted Net Income for further information.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Net Product Sales Performance</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>REVLIMID<font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">&#174;</font>&#160;sales for the second quarter increased 19 percent to $1,444 million and were driven by volume in both the U.S. and International markets, increased duration of therapy and continued market share leadership in multiple myeloma.&#160; U.S. sales of $873 million and International sales of $571 million increased 22 percent and 15 percent, respectively.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>ABRAXANE<font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">&#174;</font>&#160;sales for the second quarter were $244 million, a 13 percent increase.&#160; U.S. sales of $170 million and International sales of $74 million increased 6 percent and 34 percent, respectively.&#160; The increase in sales reflects volume growth in both the U.S. and Europe driven by increased use in pancreatic cancer.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>POMALYST<font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">&#174;</font>/IMNOVID<font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">&#174;</font>&#160;sales for the second quarter were $235 million, an increase of 46%.&#160; U.S. sales were $144 million and International sales were $91 million, an increase of 38% and 60%, respectively.&#160; POMALYST<font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">&#174;</font>/IMNOVID<font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">&#174;</font>&#160;sales were driven by volume increases globally, increasing duration of treatment and share gains, as well as geographic expansion, including the launch in Japan in June.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>VIDAZA<font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">&#174;</font>&#160;sales in the second quarter remained flat year-over-year at $152 million.&#160; International sales were $146 million, an increase of 3 percent.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>OTEZLA<font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">&#174;</font>&#160;sales for the second quarter were $90 million, increasing 49 percent over the first quarter of 2015.&#160; U.S. sales were $85 million and International sales were $5 million.&#160; OTEZLA<font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">&#174;</font>&#160;uptake and market share gains have been strong in the U.S. since the initial approval in March&nbsp;2014.&#160; Early launch countries in Europe have begun contributing.&#160; Prescription trends continue to increase.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>All other product sales, which include THALOMID<font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">&#174;</font>,&nbsp;ISTODAX<font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">&#174;</font>&#160;and an authorized generic of VIDAZA<font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">&#174;</font>&#160;drug product in the U.S., were $89 million in the second quarter of 2015 compared to $98 million for the second quarter of 2014.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Research and Development (R&amp;D)</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Adjusted R&amp;D expenses were $477 million for the second quarter of 2015 compared to $397 million for the second quarter of 2014.&#160; The increase was primarily due to an increase in clinical trial activity across the portfolio.&#160; On a GAAP basis, R&amp;D expenses were $1,110 million for the second quarter of 2015 and $457 million for the same period in 2014 primarily reflecting an increase in upfront collaboration expenses.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade align="left" style="color:#010101;"></div>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Selling, General, and Administrative (SG&amp;A)</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Adjusted SG&amp;A expenses were $541 million for the second quarter of 2015 compared to $440 million for the second quarter of 2014.&#160; The increase was primarily due to investments in support of the global launches of OTEZLA</font><font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">&#174;</font>&#160;in psoriasis and psoriatic arthritis and REVLIMID<font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">&#174;</font>&#160;in newly diagnosed multiple myeloma.&#160; On a GAAP basis, SG&amp;A expenses were $617 million for the second quarter of 2015 compared to $492 million for the same period in 2014.&#160; The increase in GAAP SG&amp;A expenses also included an increase in share-based compensation expense.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Cash, Cash Equivalents, and Marketable Securities</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In the second quarter of 2015, Celgene purchased approximately 7.9 million of its shares at a total cost of approximately $902 million.&#160; In June, the share repurchase authorization was increased by an additional $4.0 billion.&#160; As of June&nbsp;30, 2015, the Company had approximately $5.1 billion remaining authorization under the stock repurchase program, including the additional $4.0 billion.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Operating cash flow was $284 million in the second quarter of 2015 which included $570 million of upfront payments relating to research and development collaborations.&#160; Celgene ended the quarter with approximately $7.5 billion in cash, cash equivalents and marketable securities.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">2015 Adjusted EPS Guidance Raised</font></u></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Total net product sales are expected to be in the range of $9.0 billion to $9.5 billion</p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>REVLIMID<font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">&#174;</font>&#160;net sales are expected to be in the range of $5.6 billion to $5.7 billion</p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>ABRAXANE<font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">&#174;</font>&#160;net sales are expected to be in the range of $1.0 billion to $1.25 billion</p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Adjusted diluted EPS is expected to be in the range of $4.75 to $4.85, up from the original range of $4.60 to $4.75, an increase of approximately 29% over 2014 adjusted diluted EPS</p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>GAAP diluted EPS is expected to be in the range of $2.17 to $2.46, lowered from the original range of $2.97 to $3.19</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Key Accomplishments in First Half of 2015</font></u></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Presented results from the Follicular Lymphoma Analysis of Surrogacy Hypothesis (FLASH) trial, co-sponsored by Celgene and Roche, at the American Society of Clinical Oncology (ASCO) Annual Meeting</p>

<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Received Orphan Drug Designation from the U.S. Food and Drug Administration for GED-0301 for the treatment of pediatric Crohn&#146;s disease</p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Announced the signing of an agreement to acquire Receptos,&nbsp;Inc. for $232.00 per share, or a total of approximately $7.2 billion, net of cash acquired</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Research and Early Development</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Filed four Investigational New Drug (IND) applications</p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Initiated phase I trials with CC-90002 (anti-CD47 antibody) in multiple myeloma and solid tumors</p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Initiated CC-486 in phase II trials for metastatic breast cancer and nasopharyngeal cancer and a phase I trial for DLBCL</p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Initiated phase I trial with CC-90003 (selective ERK inhibitor) in relapsed and refractory solid tumors</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Second Quarter 2015 Conference Call and Webcast Information</font></u></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Celgene will host a conference call to discuss the second quarter of 2015 operational and financial performance on Thursday, July&nbsp;23, 2015, at 9 a.m.&nbsp;ET.&#160; The conference call will be available by webcast at www.celgene.com.&#160; An audio replay of the call will be available from noon July&nbsp;23, 2015, until midnight ET July&nbsp;30, 2015.&#160; To access the replay in the U.S., dial (855) 859-2056; outside the U.S. dial (404) 537-3406.&#160; The participant passcode is 82289992.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">About Celgene</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Celgene Corporation, headquartered in Summit, New Jersey, is an integrated global biopharmaceutical company engaged primarily in the discovery, development and commercialization of innovative therapies for the treatment of cancer and inflammatory diseases through gene and protein regulation. For more information, please visit www.celgene.com. Follow Celgene on Social Media: @Celgene, Pinterest, LinkedIn and YouTube.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">About REVLIMID</font></b><b><font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;font-weight:bold;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">&#174;</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In the U.S., REVLIMID</font><font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">&#174;</font>&#160;(lenalidomide) in combination with dexamethasone is indicated for the treatment of patients with multiple myeloma.&#160; REVLIMID<font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">&#174;</font>&#160;is indicated for patients with transfusion-dependent anemia due to Low- or Intermediate-1-risk myelodysplastic syndromes (MDS) associated with a deletion 5q cytogenetic abnormality with or without additional cytogenetic abnormalities.&#160; REVLIMID<font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">&#174;</font>&#160;is approved in the U.S. for the treatment of patients with mantle cell lymphoma (MCL) whose disease has relapsed or progressed after two prior therapies, one of which included bortezomib.&#160; Limitations of Use: REVLIMID<font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">&#174;</font>&#160;is not indicated and is not recommended for the treatment of chronic lymphocytic leukemia (CLL) outside of controlled clinical trials.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">About ABRAXANE</font></b><b><font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;font-weight:bold;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">&#174;</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In the U.S., ABRAXANE</font><font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">&#174;</font>&#160;for Injectable Suspension (paclitaxel protein-bound particles for injectable suspension) (albumin-bound) is indicated for the treatment of breast cancer after failure of combination chemotherapy for metastatic disease or relapse within six months of adjuvant chemotherapy.&#160; Prior therapy should have included an anthracycline unless clinically contraindicated.&#160; ABRAXANE<font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">&#174;</font>&#160;is indicated for the first-line treatment of locally advanced or metastatic non-small cell lung cancer, in combination with carboplatin, in patients who are not candidates for curative surgery or radiation therapy.&#160; ABRAXANE<font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">&#174;</font>&#160;is also indicated for the first-line treatment of metastatic adenocarcinoma of the pancreas in combination with gemcitabine.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">About POMALYST</font></b><b><font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;font-weight:bold;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">&#174;</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In the U.S., POMALYST</font><font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">&#174;</font>&#160;(pomalidomide) is indicated for patients with multiple myeloma who have received at least two prior therapies including lenalidomide and a proteasome inhibitor and have demonstrated disease progression on or within 60 days of completion of the last therapy.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">About VIDAZA</font></b><b><font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;font-weight:bold;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">&#174;</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In the U.S., VIDAZA</font><font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">&#174;</font>&#160;(azacitidine for injection) is indicated for treatment of patients with the following French-American-British (FAB) myelodysplastic syndrome subtypes: refractory anemia (RA) or refractory anemia with ringed sideroblasts (RARS) (if accompanied by neutropenia or thrombocytopenia or requiring transfusions), refractory anemia with excess blasts (RAEB), refractory anemia with excess blasts in transformation (RAEB-T), and chronic myelomonocytic leukemia (CMMoL).</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">About OTEZLA</font></b><b><font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;font-weight:bold;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">&#174;</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In the U.S., OTEZLA</font><font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">&#174;</font>&#160;(apremilast) is indicated for the treatment of adult patients with active psoriatic arthritis.&#160; OTEZLA<font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">&#174;</font>&#160;is indicated in the U.S. for the treatment of patients with moderate to severe plaque psoriasis who are candidates for phototherapy or systemic therapy.</p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Celgene Corporation and Subsidiaries</font></b></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Condensed Consolidated Statements of Income</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">In addition to financial information prepared in accordance with U.S. GAAP, this press release also contains adjusted financial measures that we believe provide investors and management with supplemental information relating to operating performance and trends that facilitate comparisons between periods and with respect to projected information. These adjusted financial measures are non-GAAP and should be considered in addition to, but not as a substitute for, the information prepared in accordance with U.S. GAAP. We typically exclude certain GAAP items that management does not believe affect our basic operations and that do not meet the GAAP definition of unusual or non-recurring items. Other companies may define these measures in different ways.</font></i></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="1" width="25%" noshade align="left" style="color:black;"></div>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Explanation of adjustments:</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 23.75pt;text-indent:-23.75pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(1)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Exclude share-based compensation expense totaling $147.7 for the three-month period ended June&nbsp;30, 2015 and $103.4 for the three-month period ended June&nbsp;30, 2014.&#160; Exclude share-based compensation expense totaling $276.5 for the six-month period ended June&nbsp;30, 2015 and $207.8 for the six-month period ended June&nbsp;30, 2014.</p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 23.75pt;text-indent:-23.75pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(2)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Exclude upfront payment expense for research and development collaboration arrangements.</p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 23.75pt;text-indent:-23.75pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(3)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Exclude settlement of a contingent obligation to make matching contributions to a non-profit organization.</p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 23.75pt;text-indent:-23.75pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(4)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Exclude amortization of intangible assets acquired in the acquisitions of Pharmion Corp., Gloucester Pharmaceuticals,&nbsp;Inc. (Gloucester), Abraxis BioScience Inc. (Abraxis) and Celgene Avilomics Research,&nbsp;Inc. (Avila).</p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 23.75pt;text-indent:-23.75pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(5)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Exclude changes in the fair value of contingent consideration related to the acquisitions of Gloucester, Abraxis, Avila and Nogra Pharma Limited.</p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 23.75pt;text-indent:-23.75pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(6)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Net income tax adjustments reflect the estimated tax effect of the above adjustments and the impact of certain other non-operating tax adjustments, including the effects of acquisition related matters, adjustments to the amount of unrecognized tax benefits, adjustments related to the gain on the sale of an equity investment and nonrecurring items connected with the launch of new products.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 23.75pt;text-indent:-23.75pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 5.05pt;text-indent:-5.05pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">- OTEZLA</font><font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">&#174;</font>&nbsp;was approved in the U.S. for Psoriatic   Arthritis in March&nbsp;2014 and approved in the U.S. for Psoriasis in   September&nbsp;2014. OTEZLA<font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">&#174;</font>&nbsp;was approved for Psoriatic Arthritis and   Plaque Psoriasis in the EU in January&nbsp;2015.</p>    </td>   </tr>  </table>
